[维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告（2022年6月30日）第81期（共 1353人）（一）](https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/202263081-1353.html)
------

<div>
<p><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12pt;"><span></span></span></p><a name='more'></a>&nbsp;<p></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告由维权网信息中心统计、撰写与发布</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;</span><b>2022</b></span><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">（共<span lang="EN-US"> 42</span>万字。分八部分发布。第一部分<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span>A</span></span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"></span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">、<span lang="EN-US">B</span></span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> </span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">）<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">目录：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本期绪论：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">前言<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">一、本期报告概述：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">二、</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本月获悉上期名录中刑满释放<span lang="EN-US">24</span>人及狱中死亡<span lang="EN-US">1</span>人共计<span lang="EN-US">25</span>人的名单<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">三、</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本期新增被</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刑事拘留<span lang="EN-US">/</span>强迫失踪<span lang="EN-US">/</span>被精神病</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">及判刑的<span lang="EN-US">56</span>人名单<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四、本期中国大陆<span lang="EN-US">1353</span>名在押政治犯、良心犯刑期统计表<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">五、本期中国大陆<span lang="EN-US">1353</span>名在押政治犯、良心犯名单索引<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">六 、本期中国大陆<span lang="EN-US">1353</span>名在押政治犯、良心犯名单简介<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">附录：</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本月获悉上期名录中刑满释放<span lang="EN-US">24</span>人及狱中死亡<span lang="EN-US">1</span>人共计<span lang="EN-US">25</span>人的名单及</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">简历</span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本期绪论：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1/</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">几乎每个月我们都会收集到狱中政治犯们、良心犯狱中死亡的信息。由此我们可以设想一下中国大陆政治犯良心犯是在怎样的环境下服刑，而他们（她们）所遭受的虐待远非正常人类可以想象的。本期披露的被迫害致死的良心犯是</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁省朝阳市建平县法轮功学员尹国志。尹国志于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被抓捕，妻子付景遭判<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年重刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日尹国志在沈阳第一监狱被迫害致死。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2/</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">中共对法轮功的镇压仍然是持续不断，本期收集了近<span lang="EN-US">40</span>位被判刑的法轮功学员，中共对法轮功群体的镇压极其残暴且从未停止，而法轮功学员的反抗仍然是前仆后继。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">3/</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">中共当局在六四前夕对各地民主维权人士予以抓捕，崔太、徐光、王一飞、庞健、丁燕、叶洪文、卜永柱、张岳兵、孙富贵、王甘霖、张建中、王刚等多达<span lang="EN-US">12</span>位公民被刑事拘留<span lang="EN-US">/</span>强迫失踪<span lang="EN-US">/</span>被精神病。他们基本都是因言获罪，中国大陆的言论空间几乎被全部封杀。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">以上内容均记录于在本报告的各个相关部分。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">以下是本期报告的全部内容。</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">前言：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告》是维权网信息中心每月对大陆当下发生的羁押未判、强迫失踪和已经判刑的各个政治犯、良心犯案例予以汇总、统计，最终编辑和撰写了这一最新月度动态报告。本报告主要关注的对象是所有在押的政治犯、良心犯——这里包括已被判刑的和羁押未判的——所有我们能够收集到确切信息的政治犯、良心犯。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本报告竭力就包括汉、藏、维、哈萨克、回、蒙古、朝鲜、满等中国大陆多族裔政治犯、良心犯在内的信息进行收集和编撰，力求全面真实反映当前中国大陆政治犯、良心犯的恶劣的生存境遇。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告》</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月月更新，是一份关于中国在押政治犯、良心犯的动态报告。此为第<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">81</span></b>期。至此，本报告发布历时已整整六年多。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本报告为了便于人们查询检索，完全以良心犯、政治犯的姓名拼音顺序制作了完整的在押人员名录。同时，本报告仍对所有良心犯、政治犯的刑期进行了统计，羁押未判的也全部列于最后。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本报告名单人员一旦取保候审、保外就医、无罪释放、回家监视居住、缓刑或刑满释放，都将从报告正式在押名单中移除，但其简历仍可见移除时的当期附录。 <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本报告每月不辍，期期更新，其中凝聚了许多义工、信息员和编辑长期以来默默无闻的辛劳和奉献。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">六年多来，本网一共收集、整理、编辑过的有较为翔实资料的人员名单及其简历超过<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>多个<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。</b>这个数字里内涵着本网所有工作人员在高度风险下的巨大付出。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本报告之所以能够按时定期发布，并且信息越来越翔实，这也得到了大陆许多人权捍卫者的积极反馈和支持。本网对所有提供信息的朋友，在此一并予以感谢。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">六年多如一日，本网持续不断地对中国大陆政治犯、良心犯境况进行总结和报告，是为了抗议谴责中共当局以超期羁押、拖延审判、虐待折磨、殴打等各种方式对良心犯政治犯施加酷刑，而在中共狱中被酷刑虐待折磨是被关押者要经常面对的严酷现实。本网坚信，外界坚持不懈的关注，将会给狱中受难者以精神和实质的援助！本报告一直对中共当局使用各种酷刑手段迫害折磨政治犯、良心犯的行径予以的系统揭露，业已引起了海内外各个方面的强烈反响。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本网一直在及时更新、统计最新讯息，每月末发布这月度报告，谨以此表达我们对所有失去自由的政治犯、良心犯的关注和牵挂。并以此，告诉全世界不要忘记这些为自由、民主、人权而承担苦难的人们。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本网认为，本报告的定期更新和发布，可以直接反映出大陆当下的人权概况——因为一个国家的政治犯、良心犯的境况是这个国家最重要的人权指标之一。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本网</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">以此</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">揭示中国大陆当下恶劣的人权概况与良心犯、政治犯的悲惨处境，力求唤起国际社会对中国在押政治犯、良心犯的记忆，并予以持续不断的关注和呼吁，直至他们获得自由。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本网认为，定期将良心犯、政治犯的姓名和境况公诸于世，是我们能给予这些受难者以实际而有效支持的一种方式。我们深知，没有比被人们的遗忘更令这些良心犯、政治犯感到绝望和痛苦的事情。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">因此，我们必须肩负起这项工作，乃至是使命。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">六年多的风风雨雨已经过去，未来的道路上还会有千难万险，但是有你们的支持，我们仍将一如既往勇往直前！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">最后，本报告虽经本网信息中心认真核查，并得到中国大陆许多人权捍卫者协助，但仍因条件所限，无法做到适时、准确统计全部在押政治犯、良心犯信息，报告所反映的只是冰山之一角，仍然是一份不完全的报告，这需要我们的继续努力！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">如发现纰漏之处和补充信息，敬请指正，并尽可能知会本网。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">本网邮箱：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="mailto:wqw2011@gmail.com"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoListParagraph" style="margin-left: 36.0pt; mso-char-indent-count: 0; mso-list: l2 level1 lfo7; text-indent: -36.0pt;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">一、<span style="font: 7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span></b><!--[endif]--><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本期报告概述：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本期报告全文共计</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">42</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">万</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">，分八部分发布。本期报告对上期报告的所有政治犯、良心犯名单进行了一次全面的逐一核查。上期名单中</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刑满释放，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>人在狱中被迫害致死。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">同时，本期新增了我们又搜集的被刑事拘留的<span lang="EN-US">1<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">2</b></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">人</b>以及被判刑的<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">44</span></b>人，<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">合计<span lang="EN-US">56</span>人的</b>名单及简介。目前，本期报告录入发布的在押良心犯、政治犯共</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1353</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">人。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">为便于人们查询，《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯名单索引》为本报告名单的唯一索引。索引是以姓名拼音顺序排列（<span lang="EN-US">ABCDEFG....WXYZ</span>）。报告将以此顺序标准刊发每一位在押政治犯、良心犯的简介。同时，本报告对所有良心犯、政治犯的刑期进行了统计，羁押未判的也全部列于最后。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoListParagraph" style="margin-left: 36.0pt; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">为了更方便人们查询本网统计的在押政治犯、良心犯的名单，本网每期随《中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告》一起发布《中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯名单索引》。本索引将本期报告所统计的人员名单，以人员姓名拼音字母排序（<span lang="EN-US">A</span>、<span lang="EN-US">B</span>、<span lang="EN-US">C</span>、<span lang="EN-US">D</span>、<span lang="EN-US">E</span>、<span lang="EN-US">F.....X</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Y</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Z</span>）。查询者可依据姓名的第一个拼音字母，即可查询到相关人员姓名，而其简介均可在报告中查找到。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk55009291;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">如您获知有未上名单的政治犯良心犯的境况，请随时向我们知会，<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">联系邮箱：<span lang="EN-US">wqw2011@gmail.com<o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk55009291;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1353</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">名在押政治犯、良心犯名单简介<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">A.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">阿布都热扎克•沙依木（维）、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿布杜热扎克•夏木西丁（维吾尔）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿布拉江·阿乌提·阿有普（<span lang="EN-US">Ablajan Awut Ayup</span>）<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿尔恒•巴杂尔别克（哈萨克）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿里木江•依米提（维吾尔）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿斯哈·阿孜提别克（哈）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阿提开姆•茹孜</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿旺觉尼（藏）、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阿旺益西（藏）</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、阿吾勒别克·努尔加合蒲（哈萨克）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿亚桑扎（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">艾朝玉、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">艾则孜•艾买提（维）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">安然、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">安彦魁</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、昂扎（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">奥坎（哈萨克）、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">敖启珍</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">阿布都热扎克·沙依木</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">：</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">1957</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">月出生，新疆维吾尔自治区阿克苏地区柯坪县人，维吾尔族名：</span><span style="font-family: &quot;MS Gothic&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;MS Gothic&quot;;">‎</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">Abdurazaq Sayim ئابدۇرازاق سايىم</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">，新疆乌鲁木齐市新城区北京路街道中英公小区居民，中共党员，公职人员，早期曾为新疆自治区教育厅工农教育处、自治区成人招生办和自治区招生办干事，后任自治区招生办副主任、新疆教育报刊社副总编、阿克苏地区温宿县委副书记、自治区教委勤工俭学办主任，原新疆教育出版社党委副书记、社长、副总编，原新疆社会科学院党委委员、副院长，以沙塔尔·沙吾提为首的分裂国家犯罪集团的要犯之一，中共新疆当局指称的“双面人”，中国在押政治犯。自</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">2016</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">年以来，因中共新疆当局对维吾尔族等各少数族裔实行更严格的高压管控，其虽长期就职于当局任命的高级公职岗位上，但依然为中共新疆当局视为可猜疑得异己，暗中监控，收集欲打压资料；</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">2016</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">29</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">日，其被新疆维吾尔自治区纪委突然以涉嫌严重违纪为由停职工作，接受组织调查；</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">2</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">25</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">日，经新疆自治区党委批准，准予自治区纪委对其严重违纪问题进行立案审查；后其被很快开除党籍、开除公职（即“双开”）和收缴违纪所得，且自治区纪委将其涉嫌犯罪问题及线索移送至新疆维吾尔自治区检察院处置；同年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">日，其案被自治区检察院以涉嫌“受贿罪”立案侦查，并采取强制措施，指控其因十数年“严重违反政治纪律；严重违反廉洁纪律，收受礼金”和“严重违反国家法律法规，利用职权或者地位形成的便利条件，通过直接安排或向他人打招呼的方式，在企业经营、承揽工程等方面为他人谋取利益，索要、收受巨额财物”，故而涉嫌犯罪，应予批捕；后被又追加罪责，认定其为“以沙塔尔·沙吾提为首的分裂国家犯罪集团”的要犯之一，提起公诉；</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">月，其一行多人案在新疆维吾尔自治区乌鲁木齐市法院开庭审理，最终其被以“受贿罪”、“分裂国家政权罪”等多项罪名判处无期徒刑；其等不服判决，立即上诉，最高法院已驳回上诉，维持原判；截至目前，一直无法获取其具体信息。目前服刑地址不明。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">阿布杜热扎克•夏木西丁（维吾尔）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1970</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊宁市人，伊宁市克拜克玉孜村农民，曾当过木工，维吾尔名<span lang="EN-US">Abdurazzak Shamseden</span>，新疆著名持不同政见者。<span lang="EN-US">1994</span>年曾因其胞弟萨迪尔丁·夏木西丁<span lang="EN-US">(Sadirdin Shamseden)</span>发起一个旨在解决维吾尔人酗酒及毒品泛滥等社会问题的民间草根运动（又叫“麦西莱普活动”），其亦参与其中。尽管几年间该运动发展日益壮大，覆盖了几乎整个伊宁周边地区，但终因碰触到中共高层的敏感神经，引起中共新疆当局的极度恐慌，遂遭强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年麦西莱普活动被政府明令禁止；<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日新疆伊宁发生维吾尔族市民大规模抗议游行示威，虽被很快强力镇压，但之后伊宁地区的胡迪亚玉孜村又发生了警民冲突，且又有六人被军警枪杀，因其外甥哈穆提•莫哈买提<span lang="EN-US">(Hemmat Muhemmet)</span>是警民冲突中死亡青年之一，所以其亦被怀疑参与其中。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被当局抓捕，并被指控与<span lang="EN-US">2.5</span>伊宁抗议示威及本次警民冲突有关；<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月其被伊宁市中级法院以“分裂国家罪”判处无期徒刑，剥夺政治权利终身；其不服上诉，二审后依然维持原判；据悉其惨遭刑讯逼供和极端非人待遇；审讯和审判期间，几乎所有人道权利及法律基本权利均被剥夺，既无任何法律代理，又不准与家属见面，其家属不仅没有接到审判日通知，判决书中也无确切审判日期，亲属只是在上诉截止日前三天，才由小道消息获此判决信息。目前在新疆维吾尔自治区乌鲁木齐第一监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿布拉江·阿乌提·阿有普（<span lang="EN-US">Ablajan Awut Ayup</span>）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">维吾尔族、新疆和田人，是极受维吾尔人欢迎的维吾尔青年歌手，因为颂歌维吾尔人而被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年被新疆当局重判<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年。目前服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿尔恒•巴杂尔别克（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">新疆伊利市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰市巴里巴盖乡人，哈萨克族，穆斯林。其中，阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，纳杂尔﹒叶尔江<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，哈纳提别克﹒萨布尔别克<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，乌木别提﹒卡斯木<span lang="EN-US">31</span>岁，哈伊拉提别克﹒木合塔尔汗<span lang="EN-US">37</span>岁，沙部旦﹒沙伊合约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，耶尔肯别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，肯杰别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，玛乌提﹒么斯尔汗约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-8</span>月，因他们分别在私下里进行了穆斯林传统常规祷告仪式，而被中共新疆伊犁市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰当局知晓后拘捕，遂很快被阿尔泰市地方法院以“非法从事宗教活动”和“从事宗教极端活动”为由分别判处<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-6</span>年不等刑期。目前各人具体判刑不详，刑至日期不详，服刑监狱不详，服刑状况及健康程度等不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">阿里木江•依米提（维吾尔）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1973</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区哈密市人，原英资企业新疆佳尔豪氏食品有限公司喀什分公司经理，曾信仰伊斯兰教，后改信基督教，喀什地区基督教传道人，中国在押良心犯。曾因在新疆喀什地区举办基督教家庭教会活动，并积极传播基督教义和发展基督教徒等，触碰到了中共当局的意识形态底线，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，被新疆喀什市民族宗教事务局认定为“<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年以来，以工作名义，在喀什地区非法从事宗教渗透活动，在维吾尔族群众中传播基督教，散发宗教宣传品，发展基督教徒”；<span lang="EN-US"> 2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，喀什市警方突然将其带走，随即以“涉嫌煽动分裂国家罪”和 “向境外非法提供国家秘密罪”将其刑事拘留，关押于新疆喀什市看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，被当地检察院正式批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，新疆喀什中级法院对其进行了秘密开庭审理，后因证据不足，被法庭退回当地警方补充侦查；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被喀市地区中级法院再次秘审，被以“向境外人员非法提供国家秘密罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，被新疆自治区高级法院重审，最终仍以<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年（ “绝密”级别量刑）维持原判。目前在新疆维吾尔自治区第三监狱服刑；据悉，在关押期间其曾遭酷刑毒打，被送进喀什农三师医院救治；其妻探监亦由每个月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>分钟探视时间减少到每三个月一次仅<span lang="EN-US">10</span>分钟；截止<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，因当地警方和社区管理部门不予开具准许探视证明，其妻探监再遭刁难。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿斯哈·阿孜提别克（哈）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1976</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克自治州人，哈萨克族，原伊宁市飞机场路<span lang="EN-US">61</span>号北苑别墅区居民，前伊犁哈萨克自治州察布查尔锡伯自治县粮食局官员，原伊犁哈萨克自治州政府移民管理局退休干部，哈萨克国籍公民，中国在押政治犯。因其曾在伊犁州政府移民管理局工作期间，接触过伊犁河流域水利工程的移民搬迁工作，熟知伊犁河是中哈国际河流和涉伊犁河流域相关水利工程项目，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月又与哈萨克共和国驻中国乌鲁木齐签证代办处副主任达尼亚尔·赛力克巴耶夫<span lang="EN-US">(SERIKBAYEV DANIYAR)</span>相结识，遂遭中共新疆当局的高度警觉、监控与强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，其已移民至哈萨克斯坦国（以下简称“哈国”），并于同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月加入哈国国籍；但<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，其被强行驾车驶入中国霍尔果斯口岸至哈国国际市场路段的哈国境内自由贸易区的中国新疆警方跨境绑架，自此失联；尽管其已移民并加入哈国国籍，但仍被中共政府视为新疆居民，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，被伊犁哈萨克自治州霍城县警方以涉嫌“诈骗罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，被霍城县警方以同罪由转正式逮捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，其案被霍城县检察院以“间谍罪”和“诈骗罪”起诉至新疆维吾尔自治区高级法院伊犁哈萨克自治州分院，指控其曾在伊犁州政府移民管理局任职期间，结识了哈国民族安全委员会成员，并按其要求对伊犁河流域水利设施及河流进行拍照，提供水利设施信息等，该行为触犯了中国法律，属于违法行为；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其被该法院秘密审判，以“间谍罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，以“诈骗罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，数罪并罚，最后执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2038</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。目前被羁押于伊犁哈萨克自治州霍城县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阿提开姆•茹孜：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1991</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区乌鲁木齐市人，维吾尔族名<span lang="EN-US">Atikem Rozi</span>，又译为阿提克木·如孜，维吾尔著名学者伊力哈木•土赫提的学生<span lang="EN-US">,</span>“维吾尔在线”网站前义工，维吾尔人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2010</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年—<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，曾因个人护照申请连续三次被当局以政治原因而拒发（尽管其无任何政治不良记录），故而将其遭遇发布于新浪微博之上，随后各大媒体，如官方刊物《都市北京》<span lang="EN-US">(Metro Beijing)</span>、“维吾尔在线”和中国《环球时报》等媒体便竞相刊发或转载了涉及其本人与其他维吾尔人申请护照时遭遇双重标准的文章，引发社会热议；此一事件因很快触动了中共当局的敏感神经，遂遭到中共新疆当局的严厉打击和报复；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，被乌鲁木齐警方以在“媒体上辩论”为由传唤，且被审问<span lang="EN-US">6</span>小时后才得以获释，两天之后又到其家继续威吓、骚扰；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，因其多次使用<span lang="EN-US">twitter,facebook</span>以及新浪微博等网站发布文章和讯息，并利用网媒广泛寻找被失踪多日的男友、维吾尔人权捍卫者穆塔力普•伊明，随被以背景是维吾尔著名学者伊力哈木•土赫提在北京的学生、曾是“维吾尔在线”网站义工为罪由被北京市警方传唤，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日其等<span lang="EN-US">8</span>人被以涉嫌“分裂国家罪” 统一刑拘（但据官方报道，其于<span lang="EN-US">2014 </span>年<span lang="EN-US">1 </span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被拘留）；同年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，因其案被定为“分裂国家犯罪集团案”，故被新疆乌鲁木齐市检察院正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月后，其一行<span lang="EN-US">8</span>人案在乌鲁木齐巿中级法院一起开庭受审；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>人终被乌鲁木齐巿中级法院统一宣判<span lang="EN-US">3-8</span>年不等刑期；其中，其被以“分裂主义罪”和“危害国家安全罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，理应刑满释放，但据中国环球电视网（又称中国国际电视台，英文简称<span lang="EN-US">CGTN</span>）在<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月发布的一部宣传片中显示，其身着囚服出现在镜头前，故其是否如期释放，或是否被释放后又重新拘留，不得而知。目前或仍在新疆女子监狱（又名新疆第二监狱，新疆乌鲁木齐市新市区东站路<span lang="EN-US">1327</span>号女子监狱，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">830013</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/blog-post_5.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/blog-post_5.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿旺觉尼（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">出生年月不详，籍贯不详（只知藏区僧人），西藏拉萨市哲蚌寺密宗学院经师，学者僧侣，中国在押良心犯。自幼成为僧侣，并长期在西藏拉萨市哲蚌寺密宗学院研习、进修；因曾长期师从藏族著名佛学教师兰林仁波切（<span lang="EN-US">Lamrim<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span>Rinpoche</span>），成为其主要弟子之一，遂被哲蚌寺密宗学院立为经师（即精通佛教经藏的僧人，又称佛教讲经诵经的师父）；又由于其受教尊师兰林仁波切是深受藏民普遍敬重的哲蚌寺喇嘛，地位、声望及影响力并非由政府任命，因此被当局视为异己予以排挤、管控，其因与之交往甚密，故而亦成为当局长期监控打压的对象；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，因藏区发生以僧侣为主的大规模抗议示威活动，以期达到让中共当局真正实现（或兑现）藏民族“自治独立”，并呼吁准许达赖喇嘛回国返乡等政治诉求，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其所在哲蚌寺<span lang="EN-US">350</span>名僧侣亦参与其中，致使抗议行动很快扩展至整个拉萨市区及四川、青海等藏区；针对此，西藏当局很快派遣大批持枪武警予以极端管控，双方发生严重对峙与冲突，随后即有众多僧侣被抓捕，其余人等被遣返寺庙严加看守；尽管此前其并未参与游行抗议，但是，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日其仍被拉萨市警方以涉嫌“参与抗议活动”抓捕，自此长期失联；另有二名哲蚌寺好友、学者僧侣亦被一同抓捕；后被拉萨市检察院转正式批捕，罪由竟是“未能阻止哲蚌寺僧人举行大规模抗议行动”；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，在被长期羁押<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年之久后，被拉萨市中级法院以不详罪名密判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，因长期失联，其狱中具体境况均无下落。目前疑似在拉萨曲水监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阿旺益西：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1984</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，藏族名<span lang="EN-US">Ngawang Yeshe</span>，西藏自治区日喀则市人，日喀则市定日县协格尔镇查那村当卓寺（藏民称之为（<span lang="EN-US">Tengdro</span>））僧侣，公益慈善捐助人，藏族异见人士，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-9</span>月，因当卓寺僧人曲嘉旺波（<span lang="EN-US">Choegyal Wangpo</span>）到西藏首府拉萨市做佛事访问时不甚将手机遗失在某咖啡馆，后被老板交予拉萨市警方处置；但因警方在查阅手机时，发现内存其及当卓寺众僧侣与尼泊尔同乡藏僧的聊天记录，尤其是存有<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月尼泊尔大地震时，他们向那里的藏民和寺院捐款赈灾等的信息记录，以及还存有和第<span lang="EN-US">14</span>世达赖喇嘛有关的照片及相关文献等；遂立即触碰到中共西藏当局的政治敏感神经，认定这是一起与境外敌对势力勾结，利用网络通讯对国家安全构成威胁的典型案件；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，其所在当卓寺突遭日喀则市当局派出的大批武警及公安警察袭击，所有僧人均被强迫接受政治洗脑教育数天，多人遭殴打；之后有<span lang="EN-US">20</span>名僧侣（含其在内）被刑拘，当卓寺及其附近的网络被切断；<span lang="EN-US">3</span>天后，除一名僧侣因向当局抗议而自杀，其余<span lang="EN-US">19</span>名僧人仍被羁押，数月不放；后其与曲嘉旺波等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>名藏僧均被日喀则市检察院以涉嫌“跟境外藏人联系、赈济尼泊尔地震，或拥有和达赖喇嘛有关照片或文献”为罪由予以批捕，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日获悉，其已被西藏自治区日喀则市中级法院以“危害国家安全罪” 枉法判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月；其余三名僧侣亦被以同罪名分别重判<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-17</span>年不等。目前疑似在拉萨市札基监狱服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/5.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/5.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿吾勒别克·努尔加合蒲（哈萨克）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1978</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克自治州人，哈萨克族名<span lang="EN-US">Ayelbek Nurzhahp</span>，伊犁州昭苏县阿克达拉镇清真寺伊玛目（即宗教仪式领祷人或主持），中国在押良心犯。早年曾就读于伊犁特克斯县宗教学校，毕业后被官方指定为昭苏县清真寺的伊玛目（即宗教仪式领祷人或主持），管辖服务于当地<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个清真寺；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，曾多次到哈萨克共和国（简称哈国）访问；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，曾因感觉新疆政治气氛欠佳而将妻子和两个孩子送到哈国，其本人亦打算将自己在新疆的不动产（包括牲畜等）变卖后移民哈国，不料被中共新疆当局知晓，遂被警方以“不准移民哈国”为由抓捕，并遭威胁让其全家（含其妻子和孩子）务必返回国内生活；其全家虽按要求照办，但<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日仍被昭苏县警方突然抓走，并被关押在当地的政治再教育营；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，被昭苏县警方以“全家要移民哈国”为罪由正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，知其被伊犁哈萨克自治州昭苏县法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">25</span>年，罪名不详，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2042</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日；据悉，在被判决时，法院竟称让其“自己选择罪名，然后给判刑”；其妻、其弟被送政治再教育营教育，后亦被以同罪由各判<span lang="EN-US">18</span>年。目前在生产建设兵团农七师高泉监狱（新疆伊犁哈萨克自治州奎屯市，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">833200</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿亚桑扎（藏族）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">青海省果洛州牧民。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿亚桑扎是因为上访被抓捕的，<span lang="EN-US"> 2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月份，因为他经牧民选举当上牧委会主任，却被官方把<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年已经了结的案件，重新拿出来说事把他抓捕冤屈判刑一年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，上诉也被维持原判。阿亚桑扎<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日下午在果洛州高速路口上访途中，被公安人员抓捕连夜送到西宁次日送到了乐都区看守所。阿亚桑扎对自己被关押到离果洛州<span lang="EN-US">600</span>公里外的看守所感到不可理解，认为这是官方对他的一种折磨。他被抓时正在带领大家控告相关人员贪污犯罪的事情进展情况，要大家继续坚持控告下去。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，阿亚桑扎被当局判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年有期徒刑。阿亚桑扎等所谓涉恶案件开庭两天当庭宣判，其对获刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年当庭表示不服提起上诉。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">艾朝玉<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">成都市法轮功学员。刘伟、艾朝玉夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被成都公安局成华分局国保、双水碾派出所警察抄家并抓捕。刘伟、艾朝玉夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被成华区公安分局批捕，关押在郫县看守所。构陷他们的所谓「案件」曾两次退回侦查机关。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，成华区检察院把刘伟、艾朝玉夫妇起诉到成华区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日下午，刘伟、艾朝玉夫妇，在成都市成华区法院一楼视频开庭，分别被判刑八年。庭审结束后，夫妻俩与家人坚决不服判决，马上要求上诉，并请律师继续代理二审。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">艾则孜•艾买提（维吾尔）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">47</span>岁，新疆阿克苏地区维族教长。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月因皮山县一个村市集从事宗教教学活动，被当地公安局拘捕，同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被判入狱<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">安然：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">本名崔浩新、济南回民作家、诗人（即推友<span lang="EN-US">@ismaelan </span>）。安然现年<span lang="EN-US">41</span>岁的安然曾在官方刊物发表过自己的作品，其中有作品被收录到中国作家协会编选的“新时期少数民族文学选”。他早前发表的《我的诗歌志》，记录其诗歌生涯中有一大部分为关注新疆的内容。此前<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月曾因在推特转发和发布的有关新疆“再教育营”的报道和文字等言论遭警方抓捕，后都有惊无险获释。于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日即农历春节除夕夜遭济南警方刑事拘留，罪名是寻衅滋事。目前音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">安彦魁：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">基督徒，山西郇城归正教会传道。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，安彦魁传道和张乘豪被山西汾阳的吕梁县公安局带走，似与此前汾阳五位基督教徒被以“偷越边境罪”刑拘、逮捕一案有关。安彦魁、张乘豪和汾阳五位基督教徒都曾在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月底，到马来西亚亚吉隆坡参加唐崇荣牧师组织的“<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>福音与文化大会”。当时他们都是持护照从海关正常出入，并无违法行为。后教会五位弟兄于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日上午被刑事拘留，被抓捕的理由竟然是“偷越边境”。后安彦魁传道于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被汾阳市公安局以涉嫌偷越国境罪刑事拘留，现羁押在孝义市看守所。安彦魁传道被刑事拘留后，其妻子姚聪娅表示：“<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年年初，安彦魁拿着中华人民共和国给办理的护照，和合法签证手续去了马来西亚，连走带回顶多一周的时间。发这个信息为的是大家为我们家能有更多祷告，也是安慰为我们挂心的亲人。更想警戎周围的亲人朋友们出国游玩要警慎，免得哪天也被定个什么偷越罪……”<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/blog-post_59.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/blog-post_59.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">昂扎（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1960</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，西藏自治区那曲地区比如县人，原比如镇孟庆村干部，政治异议人士，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年以来，一直担任那曲地区比如镇孟庆村的村干部；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，因中共当局在其所在县各乡村展开‘爱国再教育运动’，并强迫藏民在各家屋顶上悬挂五星红旗，此举引起比如县农牧民、学生、僧人、尼姑、作家、歌手等各类人士的同声抗议，并发起连串示威活动，成为继<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年后在西藏自治区内最大的示威抗议活动，随引发中共当局的极度恐惧，将比如县视为极不稳定地区，曾先后集结大批军警实施“维稳”，肆意拘捕僧俗藏人，对当地有影响力的藏人处以重刑，并采取‘对内严厉打击示威民众，对外严密封锁消息’等严打措施；在此背景下，昂扎所在孟庆村的藏民亦因参与了公开抗议与示威活动，遂遭致当局的严酷打压，于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被当地警方以涉嫌“参与抗议示威”，“秘密组织相关人员在家里召开会议”等罪由刑拘，后被正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，被当地法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罪名不详。目前在西藏自治区一家监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">奥坎（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">出生不详，新疆维吾尔自治区阿尔泰地区人，哈萨克族，穆斯林，伊犁哈萨克自治州阿尔泰地区哈巴河县清真寺阿訇（即伊斯兰宗教事务主持人），伊斯兰知名宗教领袖，中国在押良心犯。近年来，因新疆地区局势日益紧张，中共当局加强了对新疆各民族在宗教信仰上的高压管控手段和措施，哈萨克族人也不例外；这期间，因奥坎是阿尔泰地区哈萨克族群中知名宗教界领袖，影响力大，遂当局严密监控，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年又因其按照本民族及宗教习俗为死者做了传统的祷告仪式，被当地警方偷拍，随后即以此问罪，被抓刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月初，其被阿尔泰地区哈巴河县法院以不具名罪名秘判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。目前羁押或服刑地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">敖启珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川泸州市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日早上，四川泸州市法轮功学员敖启珍、唐祖群、彭昭群、章兴连四人从各自家中被抓捕，随后被抄家，关押看守所，被江阳区法院起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，泸州市江阳区法院以惯用的诬陷罪名对四人判刑：唐祖群、敖启珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，勒索罚金一万元；彭昭群、章兴连被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，勒索罚金八千元。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，泸州市中级法院对唐祖群、敖启珍、章兴连、彭昭群四名法轮功学员，下达维持泸州市江阳区法院一审原判的裁定。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/19/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%89%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B9%9D%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-440219.html#2231821424-13"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/19/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%89%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B9%9D%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-440219.html#2231821424-13</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体;
